## Anti-Pattern: plan_drift
- Task: test task
- Agent: supervisor
- What happened: drifted
- Suggestion: check first
- Severity: medium
- Date: 2026-06-05

## Anti-Pattern: plan_drift
- Task: 检查现有文件内容
- Agent: direct
- What happened: 用户请求是搜索业内现有agent框架并生成对比文档，但计划的第一步是检查现有文件。虽然这符合'check first'原则，但计划没有包含用户实际请求的搜索和生成步骤，而是假设文件可能已存在且最新。如果文件不存在或不完整，计划没有后续步骤来处理原始请求。
- Suggestion: 计划应明确包含处理原始请求的步骤，即使检查现有文件是合理的。例如：1) 检查现有文件；2) 如果文件不满足需求，则执行搜索和研究；3) 生成或更新文档。
- Severity: low
- Date: 2026-06-06

## Anti-Pattern: agent_confusion
- Task: The `direct` agent was tasked with providing a comprehensive, multi-point explanation about handling prime numbers in programming, which resembles the work of a specialized `explainer` or `educator` agent.
- Agent: direct
- What happened: The `direct` agent's role is typically to execute simple, direct actions or provide concise answers. In this session, it was assigned a complex, structured explanation task covering algorithm selection, edge cases, performance, common errors, and applications. This is a knowledge-intensive, pedagogical task that goes beyond a simple 'direct' response.
- Suggestion: For complex explanatory tasks, consider using a specialized agent (e.g., `explainer`, `educator`, or `researcher`) designed to handle structured knowledge dissemination. Reserve the `direct` agent for truly straightforward, single-step actions or very brief clarifications.
- Severity: low
- Date: 2026-06-07

## Anti-Pattern: plan_drift
- Task: The plan specified a single, overly broad step for the `direct` agent.
- Agent: planner
- What happened: The reasoning stated the problem was "simple" and "不需要多步研究或验证" (does not require multi-step research or verification), but the planned task for the `direct` agent was itself a multi-faceted, in-depth explanation requiring the synthesis of several distinct topics. This is a contradiction: the task is treated as simple in the reasoning, but the planned step is complex and comprehensive, drifting from the stated simplicity.
- Suggestion: Align the plan's complexity with the reasoning. If the task is deemed simple, the plan should reflect that with a truly simple, focused step. If the user's question inherently requires a comprehensive answer, the reasoning should acknowledge that, and the plan could be structured into clearer, more logical sub-steps (e.g., 'Explain core algorithm choice' -> 'Detail edge case handling') even if assigned to one capable agent.
- Severity: low
- Date: 2026-06-07

## Anti-Pattern: task_overlap
- Task: researcher and verifier performed similar verification work
- Agent: researcher, verifier
- What happened: The researcher's task was to search for coverage data, which included checking for tool configuration in files like `requirements.txt` and `pyproject.toml`. The verifier's task was then to verify the same facts (e.g., "验证覆盖率工具是否确实在项目依赖中"). The execution results show both agents reported on the same files (`requirements.txt`, `pyproject.toml`, `pytest.ini`), indicating redundant work.
- Suggestion: Refine the plan to separate responsibilities clearly. The researcher should focus on discovery and initial data collection (e.g., running commands, finding files). The verifier should focus on cross-validation and consistency checks (e.g., does the command output match the file structure? Are the percentages plausible?). Avoid having the verifier re-do the same file checks the researcher already performed.
- Severity: low
- Date: 2026-06-07

## Anti-Pattern: plan_drift
- Task: Plan included a step that was not fully executed, making later dependent steps potentially invalid
- Agent: researcher
- What happened: The researcher's task was to run a coverage command (e.g., `pytest --cov`) and capture the output. However, the provided execution result for the researcher is truncated and does not show the actual coverage percentage, list of covered files, or the command output. The report only mentions the tool and configuration files. Without this critical data (coverage percentage), the subsequent verifier and analyst tasks cannot be properly completed, as they depend on verified coverage data.
- Suggestion: Ensure each step in the plan produces the complete, required output before proceeding. The system should validate that the researcher's output contains the specified elements (coverage percentage, file list) before the plan is approved for the next step. Alternatively, the plan should include a contingency step if the command fails or returns no data.
- Severity: high
- Date: 2026-06-07

## Anti-Pattern: error_cascade
- Task: Incomplete output from researcher leads to useless work for subsequent agents
- Agent: verifier, analyst
- What happened: Because the researcher did not provide the actual coverage metrics (percentage, file list) in its result, the verifier cannot properly "确认覆盖率命令输出是否与项目实际测试结构一致" or check for misinterpretations of coverage data. The verifier's output only confirms the tool's presence, not the data itself. The analyst, which depends on the verifier, will therefore lack the necessary data to generate a meaningful analysis report with coverage summaries and low-coverage modules.
- Suggestion: Implement a validation gate between steps. The plan's approval or the context passed to dependent agents should be contingent on the previous agent producing the key data points specified in its task. If critical data is missing, the plan should be re-evaluated or a corrective step (e.g., re-running the researcher with a more specific prompt) should be inserted.
- Severity: medium
- Date: 2026-06-07
